- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls

# Incident Root-Cause: Grafana Dashboard Migration Field Config Loss

## Your Task

A Grafana dashboard migration (v38) silently drops table panel field override configuration during import. Dashboards without explicit `fieldConfig.defaults.custom` lose column widths and text alignment. Trace this bug to its root cause in the Grafana codebase. Find: 1. The Go source files under `pkg/services/dashboardimport/` or `pkg/services/dashboards/` that implement the v38 schema migration. 2. The specific function that handles `fieldConfig` merging and the conditional logic that fails for missing `defaults.custom`. 3. The schema version constant file that registers v38. Report the repo, file path, function name, and the flawed conditional expression for each.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the incident domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/grafana--26d36ec.

**Note:** Additional repositories are accessible via Sourcegraph MCP tools:
- `sg-evals/grafana--26d36ec` (grafana/grafana)
- `sg-evals/grafana-loki` (grafana/loki)
- `sg-evals/grafana-mimir` (grafana/mimir)

## Output Format

Create a file at `/workspace/answer.json` with your findings in the following structure:

```json
{
  "files": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go"}
  ],

}
```

Include only the fields relevant to this task. Your answer is evaluated against a closed-world oracle — completeness matters.

## Summary

I've traced the Grafana dashboard migration field config loss bug to a **type validation gap in the frontend v38 migration logic**.

### Key Findings:

**The Bug Location**: `public/app/features/dashboard/state/DashboardMigrator.ts` (lines 659-669)

**The Flawed Conditional Logic** (line 662-665):
```typescript
let overrideDisplayMode = override.properties[j].value;  // ← No validation
if (override.properties[j].id === 'custom.displayMode') {
  override.properties[j].id = 'custom.cellOptions';
  override.properties[j].value = migrateTableDisplayModeToCellOptions(overrideDisplayMode); // ← Unvalidated value passed
}
```

The code retrieves the override property value without checking if it's:
1. Defined (not undefined)
2. A string type (as expected by the migration function)

**Contrast with Correct Backend Implementation** (`apps/dashboard/pkg/migration/schemaversion/v38.go`, lines 162-172):
The Go backend properly validates the value:
```go
if value, ok := prop["value"]; ok {
  if valueStr, ok := value.(string); ok {  // ← Type validation
    prop["value"] = migrateTableDisplayModeToCellOptions(valueStr)
  }
} else {
  prop["value"] = map[string]interface{}{}  // ← Fallback for missing values
}
```

This mismatch between frontend and backend validation causes field override configurations to be silently corrupted when migrating dashboards without explicit `fieldConfig.defaults.custom`.

The complete analysis has been saved to `/workspace/answer.json`.
